                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.35">
                        <l><label>ut.26.35</label> sārivotpalakuṣṭhāni madhukaṃ cāmlapeṣitam/</l>
                        <l>sarpistailayuto lepo dvayorapi sukhāvahaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.36">
                        <l><label>ut.26.36</label> eṣa eva prayoktavyaḥ śiroroge kaphātmake/</l>
                        <l>anantavāte kartavyaḥ sūryāvartaharo<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> vidhiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.37">
                        <l><label>ut.26.37</label> sirāvyadhaśca
                            kartavyo+anantavātapraśāntaye/</l>
                        <l>āhāraśca vidhātavyo vātapittavināśanaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.38">
                        <l><label>ut.26.38</label> madhumastakasaṃyāvaghṛtapūraiśca bhojanam/</l>
                        <l>kṣīrasarpiḥ praśaṃsanti nasye pāne ca śaṅkhake// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.39">
                        <l><label>ut.26.39</label> jāṅgalānāṃ rasaiḥ snigdhairāhāraścātra
                            śasyate/</l>
                        <l>śatāvarīṃ tilān kṛṣṇān madhukaṃ nīlamutpalam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.40">
                        <l><label>ut.26.40</label> dūrvāṃ punarnavāṃ caiva lepe
                            sādhvavacārayet/</l>
                        <l>mahāsugandhāmathavā pālindīṃ cāmlapeṣitām// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.41">
                        <l><label>ut.26.41</label> śītāṃścātra parīṣekān pradehāṃśca
                            prayojayet/</l>
                        <l>avapīḍaśca deyo+atra sūryāvartanivāraṇaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.42">
                        <l><label>ut.26.42</label> kṛmikṣayakṛtau hitvā śirorogeṣu buddhimān/</l>
                        <l>madhutailasamāyuktaiḥ śirāṃsyativirecayet// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.43">
                        <l><label>ut.26.43</label> paścātsarṣapatailena tato nasyaṃ
                            prayojayet/</l>
                        <l>na cecchāntiṃ vrajantyevaṃ snigdhasvinnāṃstato bhiṣak// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.44">
                        <l><label>ut.26.44</label> paścādupācaretsamyak sirāṇāmatha mokṣaṇaiḥ/</l>
                        <l>ṣaṭsaptatirnetrarogā daśāṣṭādaśa karṇajāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.45">
                        <l><label>ut.26.45</label> ekatriṃśad ghrāṇagatāḥ śirasyekādaśaiva tu/</l>
                        <l>iti vistarato dṛṣṭāḥ(diṣṭāḥ) salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.26.46">
                        <l><label>ut.26.46</label> etāvanto yathāsthūlamuttamāṅgagatā gadāḥ/</l>
                        <l>asmiñchāstre nigaditāḥ saṅkhyārūpacikitsitaiḥ//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate śālākyatantre
                        śirorogapratiṣedho nāma ṣaṅviṃśo+adhyāyaḥ //26//</trailer>

                    <head>saptaviṃśatitamo+adhyāyaḥ/</head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.1"><label>ut.27.1</label> athāto
                        navagrahākṛtivijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ//</l>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.27.2"><label>ut.27.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ//</l>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.3">
                        <l><label>ut.27.3</label> bālagrahāṇāṃ vijñānaṃ sādhanaṃ
                            cāpyanantaram/</l>
                        <l>utpattiṃ kāraṇaṃ caiva suśrutaikamanāḥ śṛṇu// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.4">
                        <l><label>ut.27.4</label> skandagrahastu prathamaḥ skandāpasmāra eva
                            ca/</l>
                        <l>śakunī revatī caiva pūtanā cāndhapūtanā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.5">
                        <l><label>ut.27.5</label> pūtanā śītanāmā ca tathaiva mukhamaṇḍikā/</l>
                        <l>navamo naigameṣaśca yaḥ pitṛgrahasaṃjñitaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.6">
                        <l><label>ut.27.6</label> dhātrīmātroḥ
                            prākpradiṣṭāpacārācchaucabhraṣṭānmaṅgalācārahīnān/</l>
                        <l>trastān hṛṣṭāṃtarjitān tāḍitān vā pūjāhetorhiṃsyurete kumārān// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.7">
                        <l><label>ut.27.7</label> aiśvaryasthāste na śakyā viśanto dehaṃ draṣṭuṃ
                            mānuṣairviśvarūpāḥ/</l>
                        <l>āptaṃ vākyaṃ tatsamīkṣyābhidhāsye liṅgānyeṣāṃ yāni dehe bhavanti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.8">
                        <l><label>ut.27.8</label> śūnākṣaḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref> kṣatajasagandhikaḥ stanadviḍ vakrāsyo
                            hatacalitaikapakṣmanetraḥ/</l>
                        <l>udvigraḥ sululitacakṣuralparodī skandārto bhavati ca gāḍhamuṣṭivarcāḥ//
                        </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.9">
                        <l><label>ut.27.9</label> niḥsaṃjño bhavati punarbhavetsasaṃjñaḥ
                            saṃrabdhaḥ karacaraṇaiśca nṛtyatīva/</l>
                        <l>viṇmūtre sṛjati vinadya jṛmbhamāṇaḥ phenaṃ ca prasṛjati
                            tatsakhābhipannaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.10">
                        <l><label>ut.27.10</label> srastāṅgo bhayacakito vihaṅgagandhiḥ
                            saṃsrāvivraṇaparipīḍitaḥ samantāt/</l>
                        <l>sphoṭaiśca pracitatanuḥ sadāhapākairvijñeyo bhavati śiśuḥ kṣataḥ
                            śakunyā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.11">
                        <l><label>ut.27.11</label> raktāsyo haritamalo+atipāṇḍudehaḥ śyāvo vā
                            jvaramukhapākavedanātaḥ/</l>
                        <l>revatyā viyathitatanuśca karṇanāsaṃ mṛdgāti dhruvamabhipīḍitaḥ kumāraḥ//
                        </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.12">
                        <l><label>ut.27.12</label> srastāṅgaḥ svapiti sukhaṃ divā na rātrau viḍ
                            bhinnaṃ sṛjati ca kākatulyagandhiḥ/</l>
                        <l>chardyā++ārto hṛṣitatanūruhaḥ kumārastṛṣṇālurbhavati ca pūtanāgṛhītaḥ//
                        </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.13">
                        <l><label>ut.27.13</label> yo dveṣṭi
                            stanamatisārakāsahikkācchardībhirjvarasahitābhirardyamānaḥ/</l>
                        <l>durvarṇaḥ satatamadhaḥśayo+amlagandhistaṃ brūyurbhiṣaja
                            ihāndhapūtanārtam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.14">
                        <l><label>ut.27.14</label> udvigro bhṛśamativepate prarudyāt saṃlīnaḥ
                            ssvapiti ca yasya cāntrakūjaḥ/</l>
                        <l>visrāṅgo bhṛśamatisāryate ca yastaṃ jānīyādbhiṣagiha śītapūtanārtam//
                        </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.15">
                        <l><label>ut.27.15</label> mlānāṅgaḥ surucirapāṇipādavaktro bahvāśī
                            kaluṣasirāvṛtodaro yaḥ/</l>
                        <l>sodvego bhavati ca mūtratulyagandhiḥ sa jñeyaḥ śiśuriha
                            vaktramaṇḍikārtaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.16">
                        <l><label>ut.27.16</label> yaḥ phenaṃ vamati vinamyate ca madhye sodvegaṃ
                            vilapati cordhvamīkṣamāṇaḥ/</l>
                        <l>jvaryeta pratatamatho vasāsagandhirniḥsaṃjño bhavati hi naigameṣajuṣṭaḥ//
                        </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.17">
                        <l><label>ut.27.17</label> prastabdho yaḥ stanadveṣī muhyate
                            cāviśanmuhuḥ/</l>
                        <l>taṃ bālamacirāddhanti grahaḥ saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.18">
                        <l><label>ut.27.18</label> viparītamataḥ sādhyaṃ cikitsedacirārditam/</l>
                        <l>gṛhe purāṇahaviṣā+abhyajya bālaṃ śucau śuciḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.19">
                        <l><label>ut.27.19</label> sarṣapān prakiretteṣāṃ tailairdīpaṃ<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> ca kārayet/</l>
                        <l>sadā sannihitaṃ cāpi juhuyāddhavyavāhanam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.20">
                        <l><label>ut.27.20</label>
                            sarvagandhauṣadhībījairgandhamālyairalaṅkṛtam/</l>
                        <l>agnye kṛttikābhyaśca svāhā svāheti saṃtatam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.27.21">
                        <l><label>ut.27.21</label> namaḥ skandāya devāya grahādhipataye namaḥ/</l>
                        <l>śirasā tvā+abhivande+ahaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva me balim/</l>
                        <l>nīrujo nirvikāraśca śiśurme jāyatāṃ drutam//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
                        navagrahākṛtivijñānīyo nāma (prathamo+adhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) saptaviṃśo+adhyāyaḥ

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.5">
                        <l><label>ut.28.5</label> devadāruṇi rāsnāyāṃ madhureṣu drumeṣu ca/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.6">
                        <l><label>ut.28.6</label> sarṣapāḥ sarpanirmoko vacā kākādanī ghṛtam/</l>
                        <l>uṣṭrājāvigavāṃ caiva romāṇyuddhūpanaṃ śiśoḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.7">
                        <l><label>ut.28.7</label> somavallīmindravallīṃ śamīṃ bilvasya

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.8">
                        <l><label>ut.28.8</label> raktāni mālyāni tathā patākā raktāśca gandhā
                            vividhāśca bhakṣyāḥ/</l>
                        <l>ghaṇṭā ca devāya balirnivedyaḥ sukukkuṭaḥ skandagrahe hitāya// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.9">
                        <l><label>ut.28.9</label> snānaṃ trirātraṃ niśi catvareṣu kuryāt puraṃ
                            śāliyavairnavaistu/</l>
                        <l>adbhiśca gāyatryabhimantritābhiḥ prajvālanaṃ vyāhṛtibhiśca vahneḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.10">
                        <l><label>ut.28.10</label> rakṣāmataḥ pravakṣyāmi bālānāṃ pāpanāśinīm/</l>
                        <l>ahanyahani kartavyā yā bhiṣagbhiratandritaiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.11">
                        <l><label>ut.28.11</label> tapasāṃ tejasāṃ caiva yaśasāṃ vapuṣāṃ

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.12">
                        <l><label>ut.28.12</label> grahasenāpatirdevo devasenāpatirvibhuḥ/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.13">
                        <l><label>ut.28.13</label> devadevasya mahataḥ pāvakasya ca yaḥ sutaḥ/</l>

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.28.14">
                        <l><label>ut.28.14</label> raktamālyāmbaraḥ śrīmān
                            raktacandanabhūṣitaḥ/</l>
                        <l>raktadivyavapurdevaḥ pātu tvāṃ krauñcasūdanaḥ//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre skandapratiṣedho

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.29.1"><label>ut.29.1</label> athātaḥ skandāpasmārapratiṣedhaṃ

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.29.9">

                            sakhā/</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.1"><label>ut.30.1</label> athātaḥ śakunīpratīṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ//</l>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.30.2"><label>ut.30.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.3">
                        <l><label>ut.30.3</label> śakunyabhiparītasya kāryo vaidyena jānatā/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.4">
                        <l><label>ut.30.4</label> kaṣāyamadhuraistailaṃ kāryamabhyañjane

                        <l>madhukośīrahrīberasārivotpalapadmakaiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.5">
                        <l><label>ut.30.5</label> rodhrapriyaṅgumañjiṣṭhāgairikaiḥ
                            pradihecchiśum/</l>
                        <l>vraṇeṣūktāni cūrṇāni pathyāni vividhāni ca// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.6">
                        <l><label>ut.30.6</label> skandagrahe dhūpanāni tānīhāpi prayojayet/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.7">
                        <l><label>ut.30.7</label> lakṣmaṇāṃ sahadevāṃ ca bṛhatīṃ cāpi
                            dhārayet/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.8">
                        <l><label>ut.30.8</label> balirepa karañjeṣu nivedyo niyatātmanā/</l>
                        <l>niṣkuṭe ca prayoktavyaṃ snānamasya yathāvidhi// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.9">
                        <l><label>ut.30.9</label> skandāpasmāraśamanaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāpīha pūjitam/</l>
                        <l>kuryācca vividhāṃ pūjāṃ śakunyāḥ kusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.10">
                        <l><label>ut.30.10</label> antarīkṣacarā devī sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitā/</l>
                        <l>ayomukhī tīkṣṇatuṇḍā śakunī te prasīdatu// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.30.11">
                        <l><label>ut.30.11</label> durdarśanā mahākāyā piṅgākṣī bhairavasvarā/</l>
                        <l>lambodarī <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>śaṅkukarṇī śakunī te prasīdatu//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre śakunīpratiṣedho

                <div n="31" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>ekatriṃśattamo+adhyāyaḥ/</head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.1"><label>ut.31.1</label> athāto revatīpratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ//</l>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.31.2"><label>ut.31.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ//</l>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.3">
                        <l><label>ut.31.3</label> aśvagandhā ca śṛṅgī ca sārivā sapunarnavā/</l>
                        <l>sahe tathā vidārī ca kaṣāyāḥ secane hitāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.4">
                        <l><label>ut.31.4</label> tailamabhyañjane kāryaṃ kuṣṭhe sarjarase+api
                            ca/</l>
                        <l>palaṅkaṣāyāṃ nalade tathā girikadambake// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.5">
                        <l><label>ut.31.5</label> dhavāśvakarṇakakubhadhātakītindukīṣu ca/</l>
                        <l>kākolyādigaṇe caiva pānīyaṃ sarpiriṣyate// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.6">
                        <l><label>ut.31.6</label> kulatthāḥ śaṅkhacūrṇaṃ ca pradehaḥ
                            sārvagandhikaḥ/</l>
                        <l>gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi yavā yavaphalo ghṛtam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.7">
                        <l><label>ut.31.7</label> sandhyayorubhayoḥ kāryametaduddhūpanaṃ
                            śiśoḥ/</l>
                        <l>varuṇāriṣṭakamayaṃ rucakaṃ saindukaṃ tathā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.8">
                        <l><label>ut.31.8</label> satataṃ dhārayeccāpi kṛtaṃ vā pautrajīvikam/</l>
                        <l>śuklāḥ sumanaso lājāḥ payaḥ śālyodanaṃ tathā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.9">
                        <l><label>ut.31.9</label> balirnivedyo gotīrthe revatyai prayatātmanā/</l>
                        <l>saṅgame ca bhiṣak snānaṃ kuryāddhātrīkumārayoḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.10">
                        <l><label>ut.31.10</label> nānāvastradharā devī citramālyānulepanā/</l>
                        <l>calatkuṇḍalinī śyāmā revatī te prasīdatu// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.31.11">
                        <l><label>ut.31.11</label> upāsate yāṃ satataṃ devyo vividhabhūṣaṇāḥ/</l>
                        <l>lambā karālā vinatā tathaiva bahuputrikā/</l>
                        <l>revatī śuṣkanāmā yā sā te devī prasīdatu//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśurtasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre revatīpratiṣedho
                        nāma (pañcamo+adhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekatriṃśo+adhyāyaḥ//31// </trailer>
                </div>
                <div n="32" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>dvātriṃśattamo+adhyāyaḥ/</head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.32.1"><label>ut.32.1</label> athātaḥ pūtanāratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ//</l>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.32.2"><label>ut.32.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ//</l>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.3">
                        <l><label>ut.32.3</label> kapotavaṅkā+araluko varuṇaḥ pāribhadrakaḥ/</l>
                        <l>āsphotā caiva yojyāḥ syurbālānāṃ pariṣecane// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.4">
                        <l><label>ut.32.4</label> vacā vayaḥsthā golomī haritālaṃ manaḥśilā/</l>
                        <l>kuṣṭhaṃ sarjarasaścaiva tailārthe varga iṣyate// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.5">
                        <l><label>ut.32.5</label> hitaṃ ghṛtaṃ tugākṣīryāṃ siddhaṃ madhurakeṣu
                            ca/</l>
                        <l>kuṣṭhatālīśakhadiracandanasyandane tathā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.6">
                        <l><label>ut.32.6</label> devadāruvacāhiṅgukuṣṭhaṃ girikadambarakaḥ/</l>
                        <l>elā hareṇavaścāpi yojyā uddhūpane sadā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.7">
                        <l><label>ut.32.7</label> gandhanākulikumbhīke majjāno badarasya ca/</l>
                        <l>karkaṭāsthi ghṛtaṃ cāpi dhūpanaṃ sarṣapaiḥ saha// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.8">
                        <l><label>ut.32.8</label> kākādanīṃ citraphalāṃ bimbīṃ guñjāṃ ca
                            dhārayet/</l>
                        <l>matsyaudanaṃ ca kurvīta kṛśarāṃ palalaṃ tathā/</l>
                        <l>śarāvasaṃpuṭe kṛtvā baliṃ śūnyagṛhe haret// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.9">
                        <l><label>ut.32.9</label> ucchiṣṭenābhiṣekeṇa śiśoḥ snapanamiṣyate/</l>
                        <l>pūjyā ca pūtanā devī balibhiḥ sopahārakaiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.10">
                        <l><label>ut.32.10</label> malināmbarasaṃvītā malinā rūkṣamūrdhajā/</l>
                        <l> śūnyāgārāśritā<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                            devī dārakaṃ pātu pūtanā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.32.11">
                        <l><label>ut.32.11</label> durdarśanā sudurgandhā karālā meghakālikā/</l>
                        <l>bhinnagārāśrayā devī dārakaṃ pātu pūtanā//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate kumāratantre
                        (ṣaṣṭho+adhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) dvātriṃśo+adhyāyaḥ //32//</trailer>
                </div>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.33.4">
                        <l><label>ut.33.4</label> tathā sarjarasaścaiva tailārthamupadiśyate/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.33.5">
                        <l><label>ut.33.5</label> śālapārṇī bṛhatyau ca ghṛtārthamupadiśyate/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.33.6">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.33.7">
                        <l><label>ut.33.7</label> kukkuṭīṃ markaṭīṃ śimbīmanantāṃ cāpi

                        <l>māṃsamāmaṃ tathā pakvaṃ śoṇitaṃ ca catuṣpathe// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.33.8">
                        <l><label>ut.33.8</label> nivedyamantaśca gṛhe śiśo rakṣānimittataḥ/</l>
                        <l>śiśośca snapanaṃ kuryāt sarvagandhodakaiḥ śubhaiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.33.9">
                        <l><label>ut.33.9</label> karālā piṅgalā muṇḍā kaṣāyāmbaravāsinī/</l>
                        <l>devī bālamimaṃ prītā saṃrakṣatvandhapūtanā//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate
                        kumāratantre+andhapūtanāpratiṣedho nāma (saptamo+adhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ)
                        trayastriṃśo+adhyāyaḥ //33//</trailer>

                    </lg>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.37.1"><label>ut.37.1</label> athāto grahotpattimadhyāyaṃ

                        dhanvantariḥ//</l>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.3">
                        <l><label>ut.37.3</label> nava skandādayaḥ proktā bālānāṃ ya ime
                            grahāḥ/</l>
                        <l>śrīmanto divyavapuṣo nārīpuruṣavigrahāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.4">
                        <l><label>ut.37.4</label> ete guhasya rakṣārthaṃ kṛttikomāgniśūlibhiḥ/</l>
                        <l>sṛṣṭāḥ śaravaṇasthasya rakṣitasyātmatejasā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.5">
                        <l><label>ut.37.5</label> strīvigrahā grahā ye tu nānārūpā mayeritāḥ/</l>
                        <l>gaṅgomākṛttikānāṃ te bhāgā rājasatāmasāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.6">
                        <l><label>ut.37.6</label> naigameṣastu pārvatyā sṛṣṭo meṣānano grahaḥ/</l>
                        <l>kumāradhārī devasya guhasyātmasamaḥ sakhā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.7">
                        <l><label>ut.37.7</label> skandāpasmārasaṃjño yaḥ
                            so+agninā+agnisamadyutiḥ/</l>
                        <l>sa ca skandasakhā nāma viśākha iti cocyate// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.8">
                        <l><label>ut.37.8</label> skandaḥ sṛṣṭo bhagavatā devena tripurāriṇā/</l>
                        <l>bibharti cāparāṃ saṃjñāṃ kumāra iti sa grahaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.9">
                        <l><label>ut.37.9</label> bālalīlādharo yo+ayaṃ devo rudrāgnisṃbhavaḥ/</l>
                        <l> mithyācāreṣu<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>
                            bhagavān svayaṃ naiṣa pravartate// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.10">
                        <l><label>ut.37.10</label> kumāraḥ skandasāmānyādatra kecidapaṇḍitāḥ/</l>
                        <l>gṛhṇātītyalpavijñānā bruvate dehacintakāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.11">
                        <l><label>ut.37.11</label> tato bhagavati skande surasenāpatau kṛte/</l>
                        <l>upatasthurgrahāḥ sarve dīptaśaktidharaṃ guham// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.12">
                        <l><label>ut.37.12</label> ūcuḥ prāñjalayaścainaṃ vṛttiṃ naḥ saṃvidhatsva
                            vai/</l>
                        <l>teṣāmarthe tataḥ skandaḥ śivaṃ devamacodayat// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.13">
                        <l><label>ut.37.13</label> tato grahāṃstānuvāca bhagavān
                            bhaganetrahṛt/</l>
                        <l>tiryagyoniṃ mānuṣaṃ ca tritayaṃ jagat// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.14">
                        <l><label>ut.37.14</label> parasparopakāreṇa vartate dhāryate+api ca/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.15">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.16">
                        <l><label>ut.37.16</label> narāḥ samyak prayuktaiśca prīṇanti
                            tridiveśvarān/</l>
                        <l>bhāgadheyaṃ vibhaktaṃ ca śeṣaṃ kiñcinna vidyate// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.17">
                        <l><label>ut.37.17</label> tadyuṣmākaṃ śubhā vṛttirbāleṣveva
                            bhaviṣyati/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.18">
                        <l><label>ut.37.18</label> brāhmaṇāḥ sādhavaścaiva
                            guravo+atithayastathā/</l>
                        <l>nivṛttācāraśauceṣu parapākopajīviṣu// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.19">
                        <l><label>ut.37.19</label> utsannabalibhikṣeṣu bhinnakāṃsyopabhojiṣu/</l>
                        <l>gṛheṣu teṣu ye bālāstān gṛhṇīdhvamaśaṅkitāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.20">
                        <l><label>ut.37.20</label> tatra vo vipulā vṛttiḥ pūjā caiva
                            bhaviṣyati/</l>
                        <l>evaṃ grahāḥ samutpannā bālān gṛhṇanti cāpyataḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.37.21">
                        <l><label>ut.37.21</label> grahopasṛṣṭā bālāstu duścikitsyatamā matāḥ/</l>

                    </lg>

                    </lg>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.38.1"><label>ut.38.1</label> athāto yonivyāpatpratiṣedhaṃ

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.24">
                        <l><label>ut.41.24</label>
                            vyāyāmabhārādhyayanairabhighātātimaithunaiḥ/</l>
                        <l>karmaṇā <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>cāpyurasyena vakṣo yasya vidāritam/</l>
                        <l>tasyorasi kṣate raktaṃ pūyaḥ śleṣmā ca gacchati// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.25">
                        <l><label>ut.41.25</label> kāsamānaśchardayecca pītaraktāsitāruṇam/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.26">
                        <l><label>ut.41.26</label> durgandhavadanocchvāso bhinnavarṇasvaro

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.27">
                        <l><label>ut.41.27</label> na tatra doṣaliṅgānāṃ samastānāṃ nipātanam/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.28">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.30">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.31">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.32">

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.36">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.37">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.41.40">
                        <l><label>ut.41.40</label> māṃsādamāṃseṣu ghṛtaṃ ca siddhaṃ śosāpahaṃ

                <div n="44" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>catuścatvāriṃśattamo+adhyāyaḥ/</head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.1"><label>ut.44.1</label> athātaḥ pāṇḍurogapratiṣedhaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ// </l>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.44.2"><label>ut.44.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvandariḥ// </l>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.44.3">
                        <l><label>ut.44.3</label> vyavāyamamlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ
                            divāsvapnamatīva tīkṣṇam/</l>
                        <l>niṣevamāṇasya vidūṣya raktaṃ kurvanti doṣāstvaci pāṇḍubhāvam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.44.4">
                        <l><label>ut.44.4</label> pāṇḍvāmayo+aṣṭārdhavidhaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ
                            pṛthaksamastairyugapacca doṣaiḥ/</l>
                        <l>sarveṣu caiteṣviha pāṇḍubhāvo yato+adhiko+ataḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.44.5">
                        <l><label>ut.44.5</label> tvaksphoṭanaṃ ṣṭhīvanagātrasādau mṛdbhakṣaṇaṃ
                            prekṣaṇakūṭaśothaḥ/</l>
                        <l>viṇmūtrapītatvamathāvipāko bhaviṣyatastasya puraḥsarāṇi// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.44.6">
                        <l><label>ut.44.6</label> sa kāmalāpānakipāṇḍurogaḥ kumbhāhvayo

                        <l>vibhāṣyate lakṣaṇamasya kṛtsnaṃ nibodha vakṣyāmyanupūrvaśastat<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>// </l>

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.44.7">

                        <l><label>ut.47.19</label> śleṣmātmake vamathuśītakaphaprasekāḥ sarvātmake

                        <l>ūṣmāṇamaṅgagurutāṃ virasānanatvaṃ śleṣmādhikatvamaruciṃ malamūtrasaṅgam//
                        </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.47.20">

                        <l>sarva eva ca varjyāḥ syuḥ śītagātreṣu dehiṣu// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.47.79">

                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.47.80">
                        <l><label>ut.47.80</label>
                            sajīrakāṇyārdrakaśṛṅgaverasauvarcalānyardhajalaplutāni/</l>
                        <l>madyāni hṛdyānyatha gandhavanti pītāni sadyaḥ śamayanti tṛṣṇām// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.47.81">
                        <l><label>ut.47.81</label> jalaplutaścandanabhūṣitāṅgaḥ sragvī sabhaktāṃ

                        <l>piben surāṃ naiva labheta rogān <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref>manonuvighnaṃ ca madaṃ na yāti//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasṃhitāyāmuttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
                        madātyayapratiṣedho nāma (navamo+adhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ)

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.49.21">

                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> śiśirāṇi ca/</l>
                        <l>kaṣāyāṇyupayuktāni ghnanti pittakṛtāṃ vamīm// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.49.22">

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.51.12">

                    </lg>

                        <l><label>ut.52.29</label> uṣṇāśca lehāḥ kaṭukā nihanyuḥ kaphaṃ viśeṣeṇa
                            viśoṣaṇaṃ ca/</l>
                        <l>kaṭutrikaṃ cāpi vadanti pathyaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṛmighnasvarase vipakvam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.30">

                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>vargaṃ madhuraṃ ca

                    </lg>

                            kharjūrabhārgīmagadhāpriyālamadhūlikailāmalakaiḥ samāṃśaiḥ/</l>

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.36">
                        <l><label>ut.52.36</label> cūrṇaṃ pibedāmalakasya vā+api kṣīreṇa pakvaṃ
                            saghṛtaṃ hitāśī/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.37">
                        <l><label>ut.52.37</label> kāseṣu peyastriṣu kāsavadbhiḥ kṣīreṇa
                            sakṣaudraghṛtena vā+api/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.38">
                        <l><label>ut.52.38</label> prasthatrayeṇāmalakīrasasya śuddhasya

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.39">
                        <l><label>ut.52.39</label> viḍaṅgasindhutriphalāyavānīpāṭhāgnidhānyaiśca
                            picupramāṇaiḥ/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.40">
                        <l><label>ut.52.40</label> taṃ bhakṣayedakṣaphalapramāṇaṃ

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.41">

                            puṃstvasya ca vṛddhihetuḥ/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.42">
                        <l><label>ut.52.42</label>
                            dvipañcamūlebhakaṇātmaguptābhārgīśaṭīpuṣkaramūlaviśvān/</l>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.43">
                        <l><label>ut.52.43</label> dvipālikān <ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>nyasya yavāḍhakaṃ
                            ca harītakīnāṃ ca śataṃ gurūṇām/</l>
                        <l>droṇe jalasyāḍhakasaṃyute ca kvāthe kṛte pūtacaturthabhāge// </l>

                    </lg>

                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.52.47">
                        <l><label>ut.52.47</label> kulīraśuktīcaṭakaiṇalāvānniṣkvāthya vargaṃ
                            madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam/</l>
                        <l>pacedghṛtaṃ tattu niṣevyamāṇaṃ hanyāt kṣatotthaṃ kṣayajaṃ ca kāsam//
                            śatāvarīnāgabalāvipakvaṃ ghṛtaṃ vidheyaṃ ca hitāya kāsinām/</l>

                    <head>tripañcāśattamo+adhyāyaḥ/</head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.1"><label>ut.53.1</label> athātaḥ
                        svarabhedapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ// </l>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.53.2"><label>ut.53.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ// </l>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.3">
                        <l><label>ut.53.3</label> atyuccabhāṣaṇaviṣādhyayanātigītaśītādibhiḥ<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> prakupitāḥ
                            pavanādayastu/</l>
                        <l>srotaḥsu te svaravaheṣu gatāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ hanyuḥ svaraṃ bhavati cāpi hi
                            ṣaḍvidhaḥ saḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.4">
                        <l><label>ut.53.4</label> vātena kṛṣṇanayanānanamūtravarcā bhinnaṃ
                            śanairvadati gadgadavat svaraṃ ca/</l>
                        <l>pittena pītavadanākṣipurīṣamūtro brūyādgalena <ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>paridāhasamanvitena// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.5">
                        <l><label>ut.53.5</label> kṛcchrāt kaphena satataṃ kapharuddhakaṇṭho
                            mandaṃ śanairvadati cāpi divā viśeṣaḥ<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>/</l>
                        <l>sarvātmake bhavati sarvavikārasaṃpadavyaktatā ca vacasastamasādhyamāhuḥ//
                        </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.6">
                        <l><label>ut.53.6</label> dhūpyeta vāk kṣayakṛte kṣayamāpnuyācca vāgeṣa
                            cāpi(vāpi) hatavāk parivarjanīyaḥ/</l>
                        <l><ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>antargalaṃ
                            svaramalakṣyapadaṃ cireṇa <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref>medaścayādvadati digdhagalauṣṭhatāluḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.7">
                        <l><label>ut.53.7</label> kṣīṇasya vṛddhasya kṛśasya cāpi cirotthito yaśca
                            sahopajātaḥ/</l>
                        <l>medasvinaḥ sarvasamudbhavaśca svarāmayo yo na sa siddhimeti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.8">
                        <l><label>ut.53.8</label> snigdhān svarāturanarānapakṛṣṭadoṣān nyāyena
                                <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>tān
                            vamanarecanabastibhiśca/</l>
                        <l>nasyāvapīḍamukhadhāvanadhūmalehaiḥ saṃpādayecca vividhaiḥ
                            kavalagrahaiśca// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.9">
                        <l><label>ut.53.9</label> yaḥ śvāsakāsavidhirādita eva coktastaṃ
                            cāpyaśeṣamavatārayituṃ yateta/</l>
                        <l>vaiśeṣikaṃ ca vidhimūrdhvamato vadāmi taṃ vai svarāturahitaṃ nikhilaṃ
                            nibodha// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.10">
                        <l><label>ut.53.10</label> svaropaghāte+anilaje bhuktopari ghṛtaṃ
                            pibet/</l>
                        <l>kāsamardakavātārkamārkavasvarase śṛtam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.11">
                        <l><label>ut.53.11</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ hantyanilaṃ siddhamārtagale
                            rase/</l>
                        <l>yavakṣārājamodābhyāṃ citrakāmalakeṣu vā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.12">
                        <l><label>ut.53.12</label> devadārvagnikābhyāṃ vā siddhāmājaṃ
                            samākṣikam/</l>
                        <l>sukhodakānupāno vā sasarpiṣko guḍaudanaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.13">
                        <l><label>ut.53.13</label> kṣīrānupānaṃ pitte tu pibet
                            sarpiratandritaḥ/</l>
                        <l>aśnīyācca sasarpiṣkaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukapāyasam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.14">
                        <l><label>ut.53.14</label> lihyānmadhurakāṇāṃ vā cūrṇaṃ
                            madhughṛtāplutam/</l>
                        <l>śatāvarīcūrṇayogaṃ balācūrṇamathāpi vā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.15">
                        <l><label>ut.53.15</label> pibet kaṭūni mūtreṇa kaphaje svarasaṃkṣaye/</l>
                        <l>lihyādvā madhutailābhyāṃ bhuktvā khādet kaṭūni vā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.16">
                        <l><label>ut.53.16</label> svaropaghāte medoje kaphavadvidhiriṣyate/</l>
                        <l>sarvaje kṣayaje cāpi pratyākhyāyācaret kriyām// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.53.17">
                        <l><label>ut.53.17</label> śarkarāmadhumiśrāṇi śṛtāni madhuraiḥ saha/</l>
                        <l>pibet payāṃsi yasyoccairvadato+abhihataḥ svaraḥ//</l>
                    </lg>

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.56.4">

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.56.11">

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.58.21">
                        <l><label>ut.58.21</label> purastādvā+api mūtrasya paścādvā+api

                        <l>bhasmodakapratīkāśaṃ mūtraśukraṃ taducyate// </l>

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.58.22">

                            tatrānilarujāpaham/</l>
                        <l>tṛṇotpalādikākolīnyagrodhādigaṇaiḥ kṛtam(śṛtam)// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.59.21">
                        <l><label>ut.59.21</label> pītaṃ ghṛtaṃ pittakṛcchraṃ nāśayet kṣīrameva
                            vā/</l>
                        <l>dadyāduttarabastiṃ ca pittakṛcchropaśāntaye// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.59.22">
                        <l><label>ut.59.22</label> ebhireva kṛtaḥ snehastrividheṣvapi bastiṣu/</l>
                        <l>hitaṃ virecanaṃ cekṣukṣīradrākṣārasairyutam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.59.23">
                        <l><label>ut.59.23</label> surasoṣakamustādau varuṇādau ca <ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>yat kṛtam/</l>
                        <l>tailaṃ tathā yavāgvādi <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref>kaphāghāte praśasyate// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.59.24">
                        <l><label>ut.59.24</label> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ kuryādetāneva ca sarvaje/</l>
                        <l>phalguvṛścīradarbhāśmasāracūrṇaṃ ca vāriṇā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.59.25">
                        <l><label>ut.59.25</label> surekṣurasadarbhāmbupītaṃ kṛcchrarujāpaham/</l>
                        <l>tathā+abhighātaje kuryāt sadyovraṇacikitsitam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.59.26">
                        <l><label>ut.59.26</label> mūtrakṛcchre śakṛjjāte kāryā vātaharī
                            kriyā/</l>
                        <l>svedāvagāhāvabhyaṅgabasticūrṇakriyāstathā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.59.27">
                        <l><label>ut.59.27</label> ye tvanye tu tathā kṛcchre tayoḥ proktaḥ
                            kriyāvidhiḥ//</l>
                    </lg>

                    <l xml:id="Su.6.61.1"><label>ut.61.1</label>
                        athāto+apasmārapratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ// </l>

                        <l><label>ut.61.3</label> smṛtirbhūtārthavijñānamapaśca parivarjane/</l>

                        <l><label>ut.61.4</label> mithyātiyogendriyārthakarmaṇāmabhisevanāt/</l>

                            nirṇayaḥ, anumataṃ, vidhānam, anāgatāvekṣaṇam, atikrāntāvekṣaṇaṃ,

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.9">

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.10">

                        <l>yathā snehasvedāñjaneṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu dvayostrayāṇāṃ
                            vā+arthānāmupapattirdṛśyate, tatra yo+arthaḥ pūrvāparayogasiddho bhavati
                            sa grahītavyaḥ; yathā devotpattimadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ityukte
                            sandihyate buddhiḥ katamasya <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref>vedasyotpattiṃ vakṣyatīti, yataḥ ṛgvedādayastu vedāḥ;
                            vida vicāraṇe, vidḷ lābhe, ityetayośca dhātvoranekārthayoḥ
                            prayogāt,tatra pūrvāparayogamupalabhya pratipattirbhavati

                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.22">
                        <l><label>ut.65.22</label> prakaraṇāntareṇa <ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>samāpanaṃ
                            prasaṅgaḥ, yadvā prakaraṇāntarito yo+artho+<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>asakṛduktaḥ
                            samāpyate sa prasaṅgaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣastasmin kriyā so+adhiṣṭhānamiti
                            vedotpattāvabhidhāya, bhūtacintāyāṃ punaruktaṃ yato+abhihitaṃ
                            pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa iti, sa khalveṣa
                            karmapuruṣaścikitsādhikṛta iti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.23">
                        <l><label>ut.65.23</label> (<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref>sarvatra) yadavadhāraṇenocyate sa ekāntaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā trivṛdvirecayati, madanaphalaṃ vāmayati (eva)// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.24">
                        <l><label>ut.65.24</label> kvacittathā kvacidanyatheti yaḥ
                            so+anekāntaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā kecidācāryā bruvate dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ, kecidrasaṃ, kecidvīryaṃ
                            kecidvipākamiti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.25">
                        <l><label>ut.65.25</label> ākṣepapūrvakaḥ praśnaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā kathaṃ vātanimittāścatvāraḥ pramehā asādhyā bhavantīti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.26">
                        <l><label>ut.65.26</label> tasyottaraṃ nirṇayaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā śarīraṃ prapīḍya paścādadho gatvā vasāmedomajjānuviddhaṃ mūtraṃ
                            visṛjati vātaḥ, evamasādhyā vātajā iti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.27">
                        <l><label>ut.65.27</label> tathā coktam kṛtsnaṃ śarīraṃ niṣpīḍya
                            medomajjāvasāyutaḥ/</l>
                        <l>adhaḥ prakupyate vāyustenāsādhyāstu vātajāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.28">
                        <l><label>ut.65.28</label> paramatamapratiṣiddhamanumatam/</l>
                        <l>yathā anyo brūyāt sapta rasā iti, taccāpratiṣedhādanumanyate
                            kathaṃciditi// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.29">
                        <l><label>ut.65.29</label> prakaraṇānupūrvyā+abhihitaṃ vidhānam/</l>
                        <l>yathā sakthimarmāṇyekādaśa prakaraṇānupūrvyā+abhihitāni// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.30">
                        <l><label>ut.65.30</label> evaṃ vakṣyatītyanāgatāvekṣaṇam/</l>
                        <l>yathā ślokasthāne brūyāt cikitsiteṣu vakṣyāmīti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.31">
                        <l><label>ut.65.31</label> yatpūrvamuktaṃ tadatikrāntāvekṣaṇam/</l>
                        <l>yathā cikitsiteṣu brūyāt ślokasthāne yadīritamiti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.32">
                        <l><label>ut.65.32</label> ubhayahetudarśanaṃ saṃśayaḥ/</l>
                        <l><ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>yathā
                            talahṛdayābhighātaḥ prāṇaharaḥ, pāṇipādacchedanamaprāṇaharamiti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.33">
                        <l><label>ut.65.33</label> tantre+atiśayopavarṇanaṃ vyākhyānam/</l>
                        <l>yathā iha pañcaviṃśatikaḥ puruṣo vyākhyāyate, anyeṣvāyurvedatantreṣu
                            bhūtādiprabhṛtyārabhya <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref>cintā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.34">
                        <l><label>ut.65.34</label> anyaśāstrāsāmānyā svasaṃjñā/</l>
                        <l>yathā mithunamiti madhusarpiṣorgrahaṇaṃ; lokaprasiddhamudāharaṇaṃ <ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>vā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.35">
                        <l><label>ut.65.35</label> niścitaṃ vacanaṃ nirvacanam/</l>
                        <l>yathā āyurvidyate+asminnanena vā āyurvindatītyāyurvedaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.36">
                        <l><label>ut.65.36</label>
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>dṛṣṭāntavyaktirnidarśanam/</l>
                        <l>yathā agnirvāyunā sahitaḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                                >&#x2020;</ref>kakṣe vṛddhiṃ gacchati tathā vātapittakaphaduṣṭo
                            vraṇa iti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.37">
                        <l><label>ut.65.37</label> idameva kartavyamiti niyogaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā pathyameva bhoktavyamiti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.38">
                        <l><label>ut.65.38</label> idaṃ cedaṃ ceti samuccayaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā māṃsavarge eṇahariṇādayo lāvatittiriśāraṅgāśca pradhānānīti// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.39">
                        <l><label>ut.65.39</label> idaṃ vedaṃ ceti vikalpaḥ/</l>
                        <l>yathā rasaudanaḥ saghṛtā yavāgūrvā (bhavatviti)// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.40">
                        <l><label>ut.65.40</label> yadanirdiṣṭaṃ buddhyā<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>+avagamyate
                            tadūhyam/</l>
                        <l>yathā abhihitamannapānavidhau caturvidhaṃ cānnamupadiśyate bhakṣyaṃ
                            bhojyaṃ lehyaṃ peyamiti, evaṃ caturvidhe vaktavye dvividhamabhihitam;
                            idamatrohyam annapāne viśiṣṭayordvayorgrahaṇe kṛte caturṇāmapi grahaṇaṃ
                            bhavatīti; <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>caturvidhaścāhāraḥ praviralaḥ, prāyeṇa dvividha eva; ato
                            dvitvaṃ prasiddhamiti/</l>
                        <l>kiñcānyat annena bhakṣyamavaruddhaṃ, ghanasādharmyāt; peyena lehyaṃ,
                                dravasādhamyāt<ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.41">
                        <l><label>ut.65.41</label> bhavanti cātra <ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>sāmānyadarśanenāsāṃ
                            vyavasthā saṃpradarśitā/</l>
                        <l>viśeṣastu yathāyogamupadhāryo vipaścitā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.42">
                        <l><label>ut.65.42</label> dvātriṃśadyuktayo hyetāstantrasāragaveṣaṇe/</l>
                        <l>mayā samyagvinihitāḥ śabdārthanyāyasaṃyutāḥ<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.65.43">
                        <l><label>ut.65.43</label> yo hyetā vidhivadvetti dīpībhūtāstu
                            buddhimān/</l>
                        <l>sa pūjārho bhiṣakśreṣṭha iti dhanvantarermatam//</l>
                    </lg>
                    <trailer>iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāmuttaratantre tantrabhūṣaṇādhyāyeṣu
                        tantrayuktirnāma (tṛtīyo+adhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcaṣaṣṭitamo+adhyāyaḥ
                        //65//</trailer>
                </div>
                <div n="66" type="level2" subtype="adhyāyaḥ">
                    <head>ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamo+adhyāyaḥ/</head>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.1"><label>ut.66.1</label> athāto doṣabhedavikalpamadhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ// </l>
                    <l xml:id="Su.6.66.2"><label>ut.66.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ// </l>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.3">
                        <l><label>ut.66.3</label>
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>aṣṭāṅgavedividvāṃsaṃ divodāsaṃ mahaujasam/</l>
                        <l>chinnaśāstrārthasaṃdehaṃ sūkṣmāgādhāgamodadhim/</l>
                        <l/>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.4">
                        <l><label>ut.66.4</label> viśvāmitrasutaḥ śrīmān suśrutaḥ
                            paripṛcchati/</l>
                        <l>dviṣaṣṭirdoṣabhedā ye purastātparikīrtitāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.5">
                        <l><label>ut.66.5</label> kati tatraikaśo jñeyā dviśo vā+apyathavā
                            triśaḥ/</l>
                        <l>tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā saṃśayacchinmahātapāḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.6">
                        <l><label>ut.66.6</label> prītātmā nṛpaśārdūlaḥ<ref
                                rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref> suśrutāyāha
                            tattvataḥ/</l>
                        <l>trayo doṣā dhātavaśca purīṣaṃ mūtrameva ca// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.7">
                        <l><label>ut.66.7</label> dehaṃ sandhārayantyete hyavyāpannā
                            rasairhitaiḥ/</l>
                        <l>puruṣaḥ ṣoḍaśakalaḥ prāṇāścaikādaśaiva ye// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.8">
                        <l><label>ut.66.8</label> rogāṇāṃ tu sahasraṃ yacchataṃ viṃśatireva
                            ca/</l>
                        <l>
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">&#x2020;</ref>śataṃ ca pañca
                            dravyāṇāṃ trisaptatyadhikottaram// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.9">
                        <l><label>ut.66.9</label> vyāsataḥ kīrtitaṃ taddhi bhinnā doṣāstrayo
                            guṇāḥ/</l>
                        <l>dviṣaṣṭidhā bhavantyete bhūyiṣṭhamiti niścayaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.10">
                        <l><label>ut.66.10</label> traya eva pṛthak doṣā dviśo nava
                            samādhikaiḥ/</l>
                        <l>trayodaśādhikaikadvisamamadhyolbaṇaistriśaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.11">
                        <l><label>ut.66.11</label> pañcāśadevaṃ tu saha bhavanti
                            kṣayamāgataiḥ/</l>
                        <l>
                            <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
                            >&#x2020;</ref>kṣīṇamadhyādhikakṣīṇakṣīṇavṛddhaistathā+aparaiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.12">
                        <l><label>ut.66.12</label> dvādaśaivaṃ samākhyātāstrayo doṣā
                            dviṣaṣṭidhā/</l>
                        <l>miśrā dhātumalairdoṣā yāntyasaṃkhyeyatāṃ punaḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.13">
                        <l><label>ut.66.13</label> tasmāt prasaṅgaṃ saṃyamya
                            doṣabhedavikalpanaiḥ/</l>
                        <l>rogaṃ viditvopacaredrasabhedairyathairitaiḥ// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.14">
                        <l><label>ut.66.14</label> bhiṣak kartā+atha karaṇaṃ rasā doṣāstu
                            kāraṇam/</l>
                        <l>kāryamārogyamevaikamanārogyamato+anyathā// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.15">
                        <l><label>ut.66.15</label> adhyāyānāṃ tu ṣaṭṣaṣṭyā
                            grathitārthapadakramam/</l>
                        <l>evametadaśeṣeṇa tantramuttaramṛddhimat// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.16">
                        <l><label>ut.66.16</label> spaṣṭagūḍhārthavijñānamagāḍhamandacetasām/</l>
                        <l>yathāvidhi yathāpraśnaṃ bhavatāṃ parikīrtitam// </l>
                    </lg>
                    <lg xml:id="Su.6.66.17">
                        <l><label>ut.66.17</label> sahottaraṃ tvetadadhītya sarvaṃ brāhmaṃ
                            vidhānena yathoditena/</l>
                        <l>na hīyate+arthānmanaso+abhyupetādetadvaco brahmamatīva satyam//</l>
                    </lg>
